Notice
No Legal responsibility is accepted for the publication of advertisements regarding 
change of name in the Tamil Nadu Government Gazette. Persons notifying the changes 
will remain solely responsible for the legal consequences and also for any other 
misrepresentation, etc.
(By  Order)
Director  of  Stationery  and  Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICES
	
G. Kumar, a male child born to Thiru Govindan, 19th January 1978, residing at No. 2/238, Aranmanaikadu, 
Kaligoundampalayam, 
Sankari, 
Salem-637 
103. 
has 
been 
living 
as 
a 
female. 
She 
has 
been 
granted 
an 
Identity Card No. 1862/09 Issued by the Tamil Nadu Transgender Welfare Board, Social Welfare and NMP Department. 
by this I, may be treated  as female and shall henceforth be known as G. DEVI.
Salem,	
	
  G. KUMAR	
27th January 2020.

by this I, may be treated as female and shall henceforth be known as G. NITHYA

G PRABU alias MARISELVAM
